Task instruction sent to agent 
# Fix UDP Proxy Crash on Dynamic CDS/EDS Cluster Updates

**Repository:** envoyproxy/envoy
**Difficulty:** MEDIUM
**Category:** cross_module_bug_fix

## Description

Envoy's UDP proxy filter crashes when a pre-existing cluster is updated via CDS (Cluster Discovery Service), for example when `HostSet` changes occur. The crash happens because `onClusterAddOrUpdate()` in `udp_proxy_filter.cc` inserts cluster info into the `cluster_infos_` map in a way that silently fails when a cluster with the same name already exists (i.e., it's being updated rather than added for the first time).

When the insert fails, the existing entry is left unchanged, leaving a stale `ClusterInfo` object in the map that references the old `ThreadLocalCluster`. When the old `ThreadLocalCluster` is destroyed as part of the update, the filter still holds a dangling pointer through the stale map entry, leading to a crash on the next packet.

The fix must ensure that cluster updates in `onClusterAddOrUpdate()` correctly replace the old entry in the map, in both the per-packet-load-balancing and sticky-session code paths.

## Task

Changes:
- 3 files modified (changelogs/current.yaml, udp_proxy_filter.cc, udp_proxy_filter_test.cc)
- 52 additions, 4 deletions

Tasks:
1. Fix `onClusterAddOrUpdate()` in `source/extensions/filters/udp/udp_proxy/udp_proxy_filter.cc` so that cluster updates correctly replace existing map entries in both code paths
2. Add a regression test `ClusterDynamicInfoMapUpdate` in the UDP proxy filter test file
3. Add a changelog entry in `changelogs/current.yaml` under `bug_fixes`

## Success Criteria

Code changes match the expected ground-truth fix.
Code follows repository conventions.
No regressions in existing functionality.
All 3 modified files updated correctly.

    43→void UdpProxyFilter::onClusterAddOrUpdate(absl::string_view cluster_name,
    44→                                          Upstream::ThreadLocalClusterCommand& get_cluster) {
    45→  ENVOY_LOG(debug, "udp proxy: attaching to cluster {}", cluster_name);
    46→
    47→  auto& cluster = get_cluster();
    48→  ASSERT((!cluster_infos_.contains(cluster_name)) ||

TEST_F(UdpProxyFilterTest, ClusterDynamicInfoMapUpdate) {
  InSequence s;

  setup(readConfig(R"EOF(
stat_prefix: foo
matcher:
  on_no_match:
    action:
      name: route
      typed_config:
        '@type': type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.udp.udp_proxy.v3.Route
        cluster: fake_cluster
  )EOF"));

  // Send initial packet.
  expectSessionCreate(upstream_address_);
  test_sessions_[0].expectWriteToUpstream("hello", 0, nullptr, true);
  recvDataFromDownstream("10.0.0.1:1000", "10.0.0.2:80", "hello");
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_total_.value());
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_active_.value());

  // Simulate cluster update (e.g., from CDS with HostSet changes).
  // Create a new mock cluster to represent the updated cluster.
  NiceMock<Upstream::MockThreadLocalCluster> updated_thread_local_cluster;
  updated_thread_local_cluster.cluster_.info_->name_ = "fake_cluster";
  {
    Upstream::ThreadLocalClusterCommand command =
        [&updated_thread_local_cluster]() -> Upstream::ThreadLocalCluster& {
      return updated_thread_local_cluster;
    };
    cluster_update_callbacks_->onClusterAddOrUpdate("fake_cluster", command);
  }

  // Verify we can still process packets with the updated cluster.
  // This would have crashed before the fix due to dangling pointer.
  test_sessions_[0].expectWriteToUpstream("world", 0, nullptr, true);
  recvDataFromDownstream("10.0.0.1:1000", "10.0.0.2:80", "world");
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_active_.value());
}

TEST_F(UdpProxyFilterTest, PerPacketLoadBalancingRemoveCluster) {
  InSequence s;

  setup(readConfig(R"EOF(
stat_prefix: foo
matcher:
  on_no_match:
    action:
      name: route
      typed_config:
        '@type': type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.udp.udp_proxy.v3.Route
        cluster: fake_cluster
use_per_packet_load_balancing: true
  )EOF"));

      ->resetResourceManager(2, 0, 0, 0, 0);

  test_sessions_[0].expectWriteToUpstream("hello", 0, nullptr, true);
  recvDataFromDownstream("10.0.0.1:1000", "10.0.0.2:80", "hello");
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_total_.value());
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_active_.value());

              chooseHost(_))
      .WillOnce(Return(new_host));

  EXPECT_EQ(2, config_->stats().downstream_sess_total_.value());
  EXPECT_EQ(2, config_->stats().downstream_sess_active_.value());

  // Remove a cluster we don't care about.
  cluster_update_callbacks_->onClusterRemoval("other_cluster");
  EXPECT_EQ(2, config_->stats().downstream_sess_active_.value());

UdpProxyFilter::ClusterInfo::~ClusterInfo() {
  // Sanity check the session accounting. This is not as fast as a straight teardown, but this is
  // not a performance critical path.
  while (!sessions_.empty()) {
    removeSession(sessions_.begin()->get());
  }
  ASSERT(host_to_sessions_.empty());
}

void UdpProxyFilter::ClusterInfo::removeSession(ActiveSession* session) {
  if (session->host().has_value()) {
    // First remove from the host to sessions map, in case the host was resolved.
    ASSERT(host_to_sessions_[&session->host().value().get()].count(session) == 1);
    auto host_sessions_it = host_to_sessions_.find(&session->host().value().get());
    host_sessions_it->second.erase(session);
    if (host_sessions_it->second.empty()) {

103-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully implemented the fix for the UDP proxy crash on dynamic CDS/EDS cluster updates. Here's a summary of the changes:

## Changes Made

### 1. **Fixed `onClusterAddOrUpdate()` in `udp_proxy_filter.cc`** (lines 51-56)
   - **Problem**: Used `emplace()` which silently fails when a cluster already exists in the map, leaving stale references
   - **Solution**: Changed to direct assignment using `cluster_infos_[cluster_name] =` operator, which correctly replaces the old entry in both code paths:
     - Per-packet load balancing path
     - Sticky session path
   - This ensures that when a cluster is updated via CDS, the old ClusterInfo entry is properly replaced

### 2. **Added `ClusterDynamicInfoMapUpdate` regression test** in `udp_proxy_filter_test.cc` (lines 829-871)
   - Tests the scenario where a cluster is updated after the filter has already established sessions
   - Verifies that:
     1. Initial packet creates a session with the original cluster
     2. Cluster update is processed correctly
     3. New packets work with the updated cluster info map
   - Demonstrates that the fix properly handles cluster updates without dangling pointers

### 3. **Added changelog entry** in `changelogs/current.yaml` (lines 53-56)
   - Documents the bug fix under the `bug_fixes` section
   - Clearly describes the issue and what was fixed

## Key Fix Details

The core issue was in the `onClusterAddOrUpdate()` method:
- **Before**: `cluster_infos_.emplace(cluster_name, ...)` would fail silently if the key already existed, leaving a stale map entry pointing to the old, soon-to-be-destroyed `ThreadLocalCluster`
- **After**: `cluster_infos_[cluster_name] = ...` properly replaces the old entry, ensuring the map always points to the current cluster

**Statistics**: 50 i

filter_.config_->hasSessionFilters() || filter_.config_->tunnelingConfig();\n  const auto active_session_it = sessions_.find(data.addresses_);\n  ActiveSession* active_session;\n  if (active_session_it == sessions_.end()) {\n    active_session = createSession(std::move(data.addresses_), nullptr, defer_socket);\n    if (active_session == nullptr) {\n      return Network::FilterStatus::StopIteration;\n    }\n  } else {\n    active_session = active_session_it->get();\n    // We defer the socket creation when the session includes filters, so the filters can be\n    // iterated before choosing the host, to allow dynamically choosing upstream host. Due to this,\n    // we can't perform health checks during a session.\n    // TODO(ohadvano): add similar functionality that is performed after session filter chain\n    // iteration to signal filters about the unhealthy host, or replace the host during the session.\n    if (!defer_socket &&\n        active_session->host().value().get().coarseHealth() == Upstream::Host::Health::Unhealthy) {\n      // If a host becomes unhealthy, we optimally would like to replace it with a new session\n      // to a healthy host. We may eventually want to make this behavior configurable, but for now\n      // this will be the universal behavior.\n      auto host = chooseHost(data.addresses_.peer_, nullptr);\n      if (host != nullptr && host->coarseHealth() != Upstream::Host::Health::Unhealthy &&\n          host.get() != &active_session->host().value().get()) {\n        ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"upstream session unhealthy, recreating the session\");\n        removeSession(active_session);\n        active_session = createSession(std::move(data.addresses_), host, false);\n      } else {\n        // In this case we could not get a better host, so just keep using the current session.\n        ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"upstream session unhealthy, but unable to get a better host\");\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  active_session->onData(data);\n\n  return Network::FilterStatus::StopIteration;\n}\n\nUdpProxyFilter::PerPacketLoadBalancingClusterInfo::PerPacketLoadBalancingClusterInfo(\n    UdpProxyFilter& filter, UdpProxyFilter::UdpActiveSession::onIdleTimer() {\n  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"session idle timeout: downstream={} local={}\", addresses_.peer_->asStringView(),\n            addresses_.local_->asStringView());\n  cluster_.filter_.config_->stats().idle_timeout_.inc();\n  cluster_.removeSession(this);\n}\n\nvoid UdpProxyFilter::UdpActiveSession::onReadReady() {\n  resetIdleTimer();\n\n  // TODO(mattklein123): We should not be passing *addresses_.local_ to this function as we are\n  //                     not trying to populate the local address for received packets.\n  uint32_t packets_dropped = 0;\n  const Api::IoErrorPtr result = Network::Utility::readPacketsFromSocket(\n      udp_socket_->ioHandle(), *addresses_.local_, *this, cluster_.filter_.config_->timeSource(),\n      cluster_.filter_.config_->upstreamSocketConfig().prefer_gro_, /*allow_mmsg=*/true,\n      packets_dropped);\n  if (result == nullptr) {\n    udp_socket_->ioHandle().activateFileEvents(Event::FileReadyType::Read);\n    return;\n  }\n  if (result->getErrorCode() != Api::IoError::IoErrorCode::Again) {\n    cluster_.cluster_stats_.sess_rx_errors_.inc();\n  }\n  // Flush out buffered data at the end of IO event.\n  cluster_.filter_.read_callbacks_->udpListener().flush();\n}\n\nbool UdpProxyFilter::ActiveSession::onNewSession() {\n  if (cluster_.filter_.config_->accessLogFlushInterval().has_value() &&\n      !cluster_.filter_.config_->sessionAccessLogs().empty()) {\n }\n\n  // Set UUID for the session. To avoid exhaustion, UDP sockets will be connected and associated with\n  //       a 4-tuple including the local IP, and the UDP port may be reused for multiple\n  //       connections unless use_original_src_ip_ is set. When use_original_src_ip_ is set, the\n  //       socket should not be connected since the source IP will be changed.\n  // NOTE: We do not specify the local IP to use for the sendmsg call if use_original_src_ip_ is not\n  //       set. We allow the OS to select the right IP based on outbound routing rules if\n  //       use_original_src_ip_ is not set, else use downstream peer IP as local IP.\n  if (!connected_ && !use_original_src_ip_) {\n    Api::SysCallIntResult rc = udp_socket_->ioHandle().connect(host_->address());\n    if (SOCKET_FAILURE(rc.return_value_)) {\n      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"cannot connect: ({}) {}\", rc.errno_, errorDetails(rc.errno_));\n      cluster_.cluster_stats_.sess_tx_errors_.inc();\n      return;\n    }\n\n    connected_ = true;\n  }\n\n  ASSERT((connected_ || use_original_src_ip_) && udp_socket_ && host_);\n\n  const uint64_t tx_buffer_length = data.buffer_->length();\n  ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"writing {} byte datagram upstream: downstream={} local={} upstream={}\",\n            tx_buffer_length, addresses_.peer_->asStringView(), addresses_.local_->asStringView(),\n            host_->address()->asStringView());\n\n  const Network::Address::Ip* local_ip = use_original_src_ip_ ? addresses_.peer_->ip() : nullptr;\n  Api::IoCallUint64Result rc = Network::Utility::writeToSocket(\n      udp_socket_->ioHandle(), *data.buffer_, local_ip, *host_->address());\n\n  if (!rc.ok()) {\n    cluster_.cluster_stats_.sess_tx_errors_.inc();\n  } else {\n    cluster_.cluster_stats_.sess_tx_datagrams_.inc();\n    cluster_.cluster_.info()->trafficStats()->upstream_cx_tx_bytes_total_.add(tx_buffer_length);\n  }\n}\n\nbool UdpProxyFilter::ActiveSession::onContinueFilterChain(ActiveReadFilter* filter) {\n  ASSERT(filter != nullptr);\n\n  std::list<ActiveReadFilterPtr>::iterator entry = std::next(filter->entry());\n  for (; entry != read_filters_.end(); entry++) {\n    if (!(*entry)->read_filter_ || (*entry)->initialized_) {\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    (*entry)->initialized_ = true;\n    auto status = (*entry)->read_filter_->onNewSession();\n    if (status == ReadFilterStatus::StopIteration) {\n      return true;\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (!createUpstream()) {\n    cluster_.removeSession(this);\n    return false;\n  }\n\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool UdpProxyFilter::UdpActiveSession::createUpstream() {\n  if (udp_socket_) {\n    // A session filter may call on continueFilterChain(), after already creating the socket,\n    // so we first check that the socket was not created already.\n    return true;\n  }\n\n  if (!host_) {\n    host_ = cluster_.chooseHost(addresses_.peer_, &udp_session_info_);\n    if (host_ == nullptr) {\n      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"cannot find any valid host.\");\n      cluster_.cluster_.info()->trafficStats()->upstream_cx_none_healthy_.inc();\n      return false;\n    }\n  }\n\n  udp_session_info_.upstreamInfo()->setUpstreamHost(host_);\n  cluster_.addSession(host_.get(), this);\n  createUdpSocket(host_);\n  return true;\n}\n\nvoid UdpProxyFilter::UdpActiveSession::createUdpSocket(const Upstream::HostConstSharedPtr& host) {\n  // NOTE: The socket call can only fail due to memory/fd exhaustion. No local ephemeral port\n  //       is bound until the first packet is sent to the upstream host.\n  udp_socket_ = cluster_.filter_.createUdpSocket(host);\n  udp_socket_->ioHandle().initializeFileEvent(\n      cluster_.filter_.read_callbacks_->udpListener().dispatcher(),\n      [this](uint32_t) { onReadReady(); }, Event::PlatformDefaultTriggerType,\n      Event::FileReadyType::Read);\n\n  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"creating new session: downstream={} local={} upstream={}\",\n            addresses_.peer_->asStringView(), addresses_.local_->asStringView(),\n            host->address()->asStringView());\n\n  if (use_original_src_ip_) {\n    const Network::Socket::OptionsSharedPtr socket_options =\n        Network::SocketOptionFactory::buildIpTransparentOptions();\n    const bool ok = Network::Socket::applyOptions(\n        socket_options, *udp_socket_, envoy::config::core::v3::SocketOption::STATE_PREBIND);\n\n    RELEASE_ASSERT(ok, \"Should never occur!\");\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"The original src is enabled for address {}.\",\n              addresses_.peer_->asStringView());\n  }\n\n  // TODO(mattklein123): Enable dropped packets socket option. In general the Socket abstraction\n  // does not work well right now for client sockets. It's too heavy weight and is aimed at listener\n  // sockets. We need to figure out how to either refactor Socket into something that works better\n  // for this use case or allow the socket option abstractions to work directly against an IO\n  // handle.\n}\n\nvoid UdpProxyFilter::ActiveSession::onInjectReadDatagramToFilterChain(ActiveReadFilter* filter,\n HttpUpstreamImpl::setRequestEncoder(Http::RequestEncoder& request_encoder, bool is_ssl) {\n  request_encoder_ = &request_encoder;\n  request_encoder_->getStream().addCallbacks(*this);\n\n  const std::string& scheme =\n      is_ssl ? Http::Headers::get().SchemeValues.Https : Http::Headers::get().SchemeValues.Http;\n\n  std::string host = tunnel_config_.proxyHost(downstream_info_);\n  const auto* dynamic_port =\n      downstream_info_.filterState()->getDataReadOnly<StreamInfo::UInt32Accessor>(\n          \"udp.connect.proxy_port\");\n  if (dynamic_port != nullptr && dynamic_port->value() > 0 && dynamic_port->value() <= 65535) {\n    absl::StrAppend(&host, \":\", std::to_string(dynamic_port->value()));\n  } else if (tunnel_config_.proxyPort().has_value()) {\n    absl::StrAppend(&host, \":\", std::to_string(tunnel_config_.proxyPort().value()));\n  }\n\n  auto headers = Http::RequestHeaderMapImpl::create();\n  headers->addReferenceKey(Http::Headers::get().Scheme, scheme);\n  headers->addReferenceKey(Http::Headers::get().Host, host);\n\n  if (tunnel_config_.usePost()) {\n    headers->addReferenceKey(Http::Headers::get().Method, \"POST\");\n    headers->addReferenceKey(Http::Headers::get().Path, tunnel_config_.postPath());\n  } else {\n    // The Envoy HTTP/2 and HTTP/3 clients expect the request header map to be in the form of HTTP/1\n    // upgrade to issue an extended CONNECT request.\n    headers->addReferenceKey(Http::Headers::get().Method, \"GET\");\n    headers->addReferenceKey(Http::Headers::get().Connection, \"Upgrade\");\n    headers->addReferenceKey(Http::Headers::get().Upgrade, \"connect-udp\");\n    headers->addReferenceKey(Http::Headers::get().CapsuleProtocol, \"?1\");\n    const std::string target_tunnel_path = resolveTargetTunnelPath();\n    headers->addReferenceKey(Http::Headers::get().Path, target_tunnel_path);\n  }\n\n  tunnel_config_.headerEvaluator().evaluateHeaders(*headers, {downstream_info_.getRequestHeaders()},\n                                                   downstream_info_);\n\n  const auto status = request_encoder_->encodeHeaders(*headers, false);\n  // Encoding can only fail on missing required request headers.\n  ASSERT(status.ok());\n}\n\nconst std::string HttpUpstreamImpl::resolveTargetTunnelPath() {\n  std::string target_host = tunnel_config_.targetHost(downstream_info_);\n  target_host = Http::Utility::PercentEncoding::encode(target_host, \":\");\n\n  const auto* dynamic_port =\n      downstream_info_.filterState()->getDataReadOnly<StreamInfo::UInt32Accessor>(\n          \"udp.connect.target_port\");\n\n  std::string target_port;\n  if (dynamic_port != nullptr && dynamic_port->value() > 0 && dynamic_port->value() <= 65535) {\n    target_port = std::to_string(dynamic_port->value());\n  } else {\n    target_port = std::to_string(tunnel_config_.defaultTargetPort());\n  }\n\n  // TODO(ohadvano): support configurable URI template.\n  return absl::StrCat(\"/.well-known/masque/udp/\", target_host, \"/\", target_port, \"/\");\n}\n\nHttpUpstreamImpl::~HttpUpstreamImpl() { resetEncoder(Network::ConnectionEvent::LocalClose); }\n\nvoid HttpUpstreamImpl::resetEncoder(Network::ConnectionEvent event, bool by_downstream) {\n  if (!request_encoder_) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  request_encoder_->getStream().removeCallbacks(*this);\n  if (by_downstream) {\n    request_encoder_->getStream().resetStream(Http::StreamResetReason::LocalReset);\n  }\n\n  request_encoder_ = nullptr;\n\n  // If we did not receive a valid CONNECT response yet we treat this as a pool\n  // failure, otherwise we forward the event downstream.\n  if (tunnel_creation_callbacks_.has_value()) {\n    tunnel_creation_callbacks_.value().get().onStreamFailure();\n    return;\n  }\n\n EXPECT_THAT(output_.front(), testing::HasSubstr(\"session_complete\"));\n}\n\nclass HttpUpstreamImplTest : public testing::Test {\npublic:\n  struct HeaderToAdd {\n    std::string key_;\n    std::string value_;\n  };\n\n  Http::TestRequestHeaderMapImpl\n  expectedHeaders(bool is_ssl = false, bool use_post = false,\n                  absl::optional<std::string> opt_authority = absl::nullopt,\n                  absl::optional<std::string> opt_path = absl::nullopt,\n                  absl::optional<HeaderToAdd> header_to_add = absl::nullopt) {\n    // In case connect-udp is used, Envoy expect the H2 headers to be normalized with H1,\n    // so expect that the request headers here match H1 headers, even though\n    // eventually H2 headers will be sent. When the headers are normalized to H1, the method\n    // is replaced with GET, a header with the 'upgrade' key is added with 'connect-udp'\n    // value and a header with the 'connection' key is added with 'Upgrade' value.\n    std::string scheme = is_ssl ? \"https\" : \"http\";\n    std::string authority =\n        opt_authority.has_value() ? opt_authority.value() : \"default.host.com:10\";\n    std::string method = use_post ? \"POST\" : \"GET\";\n    std::string path =\n        opt_path.has_value() ? opt_path.value() : \"/.well-known/masque/udp/default.target.host/20/\";\n\n    auto headers = Http::TestRequestHeaderMapImpl{\n        {\":scheme\", scheme}, {\":authority\", authority}, {\":method\", method}, {\":path\", path}};\n\n    if (!use_post) {\n      headers.addCopy(\"capsule-protocol\", \"?1\");\n      headers.addCopy(\"upgrade\", \"connect-udp\");\n      headers.addCopy(\"connection\", \"Upgrade\");\n    }\n\n    if (header_to_add) {\n      headers.addCopy(header_to_add.value().key_, header_to_add.value().value_);\n    }\n\n    return headers;\n  }\n\n  void setAndExpectRequestEncoder(Http::TestRequestHeaderMapImpl expected_headers,\n                                  bool is_ssl = false) {\n    EXPECT_CALL(request_encoder_.stream_, addCallbacks(_));\n    EXPECT_CALL(request_encoder_, encodeHeaders(_, _))\n        .WillOnce(Invoke([expected_headers](const Http::RequestHeaderMap& headers,\n                                            bool end_stream) -> Http::Status {\n          EXPECT_THAT(&headers, HeaderMapEqualIgnoreOrder(&expected_headers));\n          EXPECT_FALSE(end_stream);\n          return absl::OkStatus();\n        }));\n\n    upstream_->setRequestEncoder(request_encoder_, is_ssl);\n\n    // Verify that resetEncoder is called only once.\n    EXPECT_CALL(request_encoder_.stream_, removeCallbacks(_));\n  }\n\n  void filterStateOverride(absl::optional<uint32_t> proxy_port = absl::nullopt,\n                           absl::optional<uint32_t> target_port = absl::nullopt) {\n    if (proxy_port) {\n      stream_info_.filterState()->setData(\n          \"udp.connect.proxy_port\",\n          std::make_shared<StreamInfo::UInt32AccessorImpl>(proxy_port.value()),\n          Envoy::StreamInfo::FilterState::StateType::Mutable);\n    }\n\n    if (target_port) {\n      stream_info_.filterState()->setData(\n          \"udp.connect.target_port\",\n          std::make_shared<StreamInfo::UInt32AccessorImpl>(target_port.value()),\n          Envoy::StreamInfo::FilterState::StateType::Mutable);\n    }\n  }\n\n  void setup(absl::optional<HeaderToAdd> header_to_add = absl::nullopt) {\n    Protobuf::RepeatedPtrField<envoy::config::core::v3::HeaderValueOption> headers_to_add;\n    if (header_to_add) {\n      envoy::config::core::v3::HeaderValueOption* header = headers_to_add.Add();\n      header->mutable_header()->set_key(header_to_add.value().key_);\n      header->mutable_header()->set_value(header_to_add.value().value_);\n    }\n\n    header_evaluator_ = Envoy::Router::HeaderParser::configure(headers_to_add);\n    config_ = std::make_unique<NiceMock<MockUdpTunnelingConfig>>(*header_evaluator_);\n    upstream_ = std::make_unique<HttpUpstreamImpl>(callbacks_, *config_, stream_info_);\n    upstream_->setTunnelCreationCallbacks(creation_callbacks_);\n  }\n\n  NiceMock<MockUpstreamTunnelCallbacks> callbacks_;\n  NiceMock<StreamInfo::MockStreamInfo> stream_info_;\n used, Envoy expect the H2 headers to be normalized with H1,\n    // so expect that the request headers here match H1 headers, even though\n    // eventually H2 headers will be sent. When the headers are normalized to H1, the method\n    // is replaced with GET, a header with the 'upgrade' key is added with 'connect-udp'\n    // value and a header with the 'connection' key is added with 'Upgrade' value.\n    std::string scheme = is_ssl ? \"https\" : \"http\";\n    std::string authority =\n        opt_authority.has_value() ? opt_authority.value() : \"default.host.com:10\";\n    std::string method = use_post ? \"POST\" : \"GET\";\n    std::string path =\n        opt_path.has_value() ? opt_path.value() : \"/.well-known/masque/udp/default.target.host/20/\";\n\n    auto headers = Http::TestRequestHeaderMapImpl{\n        {\":scheme\", scheme}, {\":authority\", authority}, {\":method\", method}, {\":path\", path}};\n\n    if (!use_post) {\n      headers.addCopy(\"capsule-protocol\", \"?1\");\n      headers.addCopy(\"upgrade\", \"connect-udp\");\n      headers.addCopy(\"connection\", \"Upgrade\");\n    }\n\n    if (header_to_add) {\n      headers.addCopy(header_to_add.value().key_, header_to_add.value().value_);\n    }\n\n    return headers;\n  }\n\n  void // Regression test for cluster update via CDS correctly replacing stale map entry.
TEST_F(UdpProxyFilterTest, ClusterDynamicInfoMapUpdate) {
  InSequence s;

  setup(readConfig(R"EOF(
stat_prefix: foo
matcher:
  on_no_match:
    action:
      name: route
      typed_config:
        '@type': type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.udp.udp_proxy.v3.Route
        cluster: fake_cluster
  )EOF"));

  // Send initial packet.
  expectSessionCreate(upstream_address_);
  test_sessions_[0].expectWriteToUpstream("hello", 0, nullptr, true);
  recvDataFromDownstream("10.0.0.1:1000", "10.0.0.2:80", "hello");
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_total_.value());
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_active_.value());

  // Simulate cluster update (e.g., from CDS with HostSet changes).
  // Create a new mock cluster to represent the updated cluster.
  NiceMock<Upstream::MockThreadLocalCluster> updated_thread_local_cluster;
  updated_thread_local_cluster.cluster_.info_->name_ = "fake_cluster";
  {
    Upstream::ThreadLocalClusterCommand command =
        [&updated_thread_local_cluster]() -> Upstream::ThreadLocalCluster& {
      return updated_thread_local_cluster;
    };
    cluster_update_callbacks_->onClusterAddOrUpdate("fake_cluster", command);
  }

  // Verify we can still process packets with the updated cluster.
  // This would have crashed before the fix due to dangling pointer.
  test_sessions_[0].expectWriteToUpstream("world", 0, nullptr, true);
  recvDataFromDownstream("10.0.0.1:1000", "10.0.0.2:80", "world");
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_active_.value());
}

4. EDIT /workspace/test/extensions/filters/udp/udp_proxy/udp_proxy_filter_test.cc
Before
// Regression test for cluster update via CDS correctly replacing stale map entry.
TEST_F(UdpProxyFilterTest, ClusterDynamicInfoMapUpdate) {
  InSequence s;

  setup(readConfig(R"EOF(
stat_prefix: foo
matcher:
  on_no_match:
    action:
      name: route
      typed_config:
        '@type': type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.udp.udp_proxy.v3.Route
        cluster: fake_cluster
  )EOF"));

  // Send initial packet.
  expectSessionCreate(upstream_address_);
  test_sessions_[0].expectWriteToUpstream("hello", 0, nullptr, true);
  recvDataFromDownstream("10.0.0.1:1000", "10.0.0.2:80", "hello");
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_total_.value());
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_active_.value());

  // Simulate cluster update (e.g., from CDS with HostSet changes).
  // Create a new mock cluster to represent the updated cluster.
  NiceMock<Upstream::MockThreadLocalCluster> updated_thread_local_cluster;
  updated_thread_local_cluster.cluster_.info_->name_ = "fake_cluster";
  {
    Upstream::ThreadLocalClusterCommand command =
        [&updated_thread_local_cluster]() -> Upstream::ThreadLocalCluster& {
      return updated_thread_local_cluster;
    };
    cluster_update_callbacks_->onClusterAddOrUpdate("fake_cluster", command);
  }

  // Verify we can still process packets with the updated cluster.
  // This would have crashed before the fix due to dangling pointer.
  test_sessions_[0].expectWriteToUpstream("world", 0, nullptr, true);
  recvDataFromDownstream("10.0.0.1:1000", "10.0.0.2:80", "world");
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_active_.value());
}
After
// Regression test for cluster update via CDS correctly replacing stale map entry.
TEST_F(UdpProxyFilterTest, ClusterDynamicInfoMapUpdate) {
  InSequence s;

  setup(readConfig(R"EOF(
stat_prefix: foo
matcher:
  on_no_match:
    action:
      name: route
      typed_config:
        '@type': type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.udp.udp_proxy.v3.Route
        cluster: fake_cluster
  )EOF"));

  // Send initial packet.
  expectSessionCreate(upstream_address_);
  test_sessions_[0].expectWriteToUpstream("hello", 0, nullptr, true);
  recvDataFromDownstream("10.0.0.1:1000", "10.0.0.2:80", "hello");
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_total_.value());
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_active_.value());

  // Simulate cluster update (e.g., from CDS with HostSet changes).
  // Create a new mock cluster to represent the updated cluster.
  NiceMock<Upstream::MockThreadLocalCluster> updated_thread_local_cluster;
  updated_thread_local_cluster.cluster_.info_->name_ = "fake_cluster";
  {
    Upstream::ThreadLocalClusterCommand command =
        [&updated_thread_local_cluster]() -> Upstream::ThreadLocalCluster& {
      return updated_thread_local_cluster;
    };
    cluster_update_callbacks_->onClusterAddOrUpdate("fake_cluster", command);
  }

  // Verify we can still process packets with the updated cluster.
  // With the fix, the cluster info map is correctly updated, allowing new packets to work.
  // Before the fix, the map entry would not be updated and would point to a stale cluster.
  expectSessionCreate(upstream_address_);
  test_sessions_[1].expectWriteToUpstream("world", 0, nullptr, true);
  recvDataFromDownstream("10.0.0.1:1000", "10.0.0.2:80", "world");
  EXPECT_EQ(1, config_->stats().downstream_sess_active_.value());
}
